	function loadFeaturedGameArea() {

				jQuery.get(featureUrl + '?team=' + RegisteredFan.getFavoriteTeam(), function(data) {
				  jQuery('#featGmBody').html(data).show();
				});
		} else {
			jQuery('#featGmBody').show();
		}
	}

</script>  <style type="text/css">
#wideCol .contentBlock .articleText p {
    margin-bottom: 16px;
    line-height: 16px;
}
#wideCol .contentBlock .articleText span {
    line-height: 16px;
}
